<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мерещиться.html>мере́щиться</a> (9762)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерещиться.html>мере́щиться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">meréščitʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:померещиться.html>помере́щиться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to seem <i>(to)</i>, to appear <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мерещиться.html>мере́щится</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>meréščitsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is dreaming</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мерещиться.html>мере́щится</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>meréščitsja</b>, što</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it seems to him that</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:померещиться.html>помере́щилось</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>pomeréščilosʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he fancied he saw</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мерзавец.html>мерза́вец</a> (5238)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерзавец.html>мерза́вец</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">merzávec</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерзавец.html>мерза́вца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерзавец.html>мерза́вцы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерзавец.html>мерза́вцев</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мерза́вка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>villain, scoundrel, rat, stinker</li></ol>

<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мьрзъкъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mĭrzŭkŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. ***мерзлота.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мерзлота.html>мерзлота́</a> (17933)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерзлота.html>мерзлота́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">merzlotá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерзлота.html>мерзлоты́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>frozen ground, frozen earth; frozen state, congelation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вечный.html>ве́чная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мерзлота.html>мерзлота́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">véčnaja <b>merzlotá</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">permafrost</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***мерка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мерка.html>ме́рка</a> (9831)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерить.html>ме́рить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">méritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерка.html>ме́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mérka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерка.html>ме́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерка.html>ме́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерка.html>ме́рок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>measure(s), measurements
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:снимать.html>снима́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мерка.html>ме́рку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">snimátʹ <b>mérku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take measurements</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:мерка.html>ме́рке</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po <b>mérke</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to measure</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>measuring rod, yardstick</li>
<li><i>(figurative)</i> yardstick, criterion</li></ol>

***меркнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:меркнуть.html>ме́ркнуть</a> (17491)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мьркнути</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mĭrknuti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mь̀rknǫti</i>. Cognate to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морока.html>морок</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">morok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мрак.html>мрак</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mrak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерцать.html>мерца́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mercátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меркнуть.html>ме́ркнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mérknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:померкнуть.html>поме́ркнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grow dark/dim</li>
<li>to fade, to wane
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слава.html>сла́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:померкнуть.html>поме́ркла</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó sláva pomérkla</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his fame dwindled</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pale <i>(before)</i></li></ol>

***мертвый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мертвый.html>мёртвый</a> (6625)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mьrtvъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mr̥twós</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mr̥tós</i>, ultimately from the root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mer-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to die</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мертвый.html>мёртвый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mjórtvyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)мертве́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)мертве́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dead
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мертвый.html>мёртвая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:точка.html>то́чка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mjórtvaja</b> tóčka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">dead center</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мертвый.html>мёртвый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>час</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mjórtvyj</b> čas</i> ― <span class="e-translation">after-dinner rest</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>lifeless</li></ol>

***мерцать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мерцать.html>мерца́ть</a> (5013)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мьрцати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mĭrcati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меркнуть.html>ме́ркнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mérknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мерцать.html>мерца́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mercátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to shimmer, to twinkle, to glimmer, to flicker</li></ol>

***месить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:месить.html>меси́ть</a> (18447)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*měsiti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:месить.html>меси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mesítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to knead</li>
<li>to mix with water <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">e.g. of clay</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:месить.html>меси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>грязь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mesítʹ</b> grjazʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wade through mud; walk in the mud</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***месса.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:месса.html>ме́сса</a> (23567)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">messe</i>. Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">messa</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Messe</i>. All from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">missa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dismissed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ite, missa est</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">go, (the assembly) is dismissed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, last words of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Roman_Rite" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Roman Rite">Roman Rite</a> of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Catholic_Church" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Catholic Church">Catholic Church</a>.

***местечко.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:местечко.html>местечко</a> (4822)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Diminutive of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mésto</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">place, (dialectal) city</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or calqued from another Slavic language. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">miasteczko</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:местечко.html>месте́чко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mestéčko</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:местечко.html>месте́чка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:местечко.html>месте́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:местечко.html>месте́чек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mésto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li>A small village or town on the territory of the former <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish%E2%80%93Lithuanian_Commonwealth" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Polish–Lithuanian Commonwealth">Polish–Lithuanian Commonwealth</a>.</li>
<li>A shtetl, small Jewish village.</li></ol>

***мести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:месть.html>мести</a> (18722)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mestì</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:месть.html>мести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подмести.html>подмести́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:замести.html>замести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to sweep</li>
<li>to scatter</li>
<li>to swirl</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to snow strongly, to blizzard
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:месть.html>Метёт</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Metjót</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There's a snowstorm.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***местный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:местный.html>местный</a> (664)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mésto</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">place</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span>, <span class="ann-pos">adjectival suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:местный.html>ме́стный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">méstnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>local
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:местный.html>ме́стный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наркоз.html>нарко́з</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>méstnyj</b> narkóz</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>local</b> anaesthetic</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> locative <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">relating to the case that expresses location</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:местный.html>ме́стный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:падеж.html>паде́ж</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">méstnyj padéž</i> ― <span class="e-translation">locative case</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
